0                                  21345              ***
                                   21346              ***  Real-Time Timing Subtask.
                                   21347              ***
                                   21348              ***  The mother task maintains a linked list of timer events
                                   21349              ***  (sorted with the shortest interval first).
                                   21350              ***
                                   21351              ***  This subtask is responsible for calling the timer event's
                                   21352              ***  exit routine when it's time has come.  Note that the exit
                                   21353              ***  routine is run under the subtask, and no CP or user stack
                                   21354              ***  addressability can be assumed.
                                   21355              ***
                                   21356              ***  The subtask can be posted because an event is ready or
                                   21357              ***  because a new event was added by the mother task.  The
                                   21358              ***  subtask doesn't care why it was posted, it simply processes
                                   21359              ***  ready events (if any) and then calculates the amount of time
                                   21360              ***  to sleep until the first event happens.
                                   21361              ***
